The flags below are stored in entity->type->default_flags and entity->type->default_more_flags.
They are the defaults that get copied into the entity when it gets created.

If you want to e.g. make all horned lizards be cursed by default, set flag 15 on it's type.default_more_flags
and every lizard that spawns subsequently will be cursed.

See flags.hpp for the flags that have already been found.
